# Welcome to Pelican Park Recreation Centre

Loading...

[ CLICK HERE TO JOIN ](/promotions/join-now)

Loading... 

## 

## Welcome to Pelican Park Recreation Centre

  
Pelican Park Recreation Centre is the premier lifestyle gym and indoor swimming pool on the Mornington Peninsula, Victoria. We cater to the needs of the entire community, ensuring that both members and casual visitors become happier and healthier.

The centre's facilities offer you a fully equipped lifestyle gym featuring a wide variety of cardio equipment and weights, a functional training area and group exercise classes. With over 50 group fitness classes a week, there is a class for everyone!

The leisure centre also has a 25-metre indoor pool, leisure pool, toddler pool with aqua play features, spa and steam facilities. Staffed by a team of exercise, aquatics and customer service professionals, we are committed to being readily accessible for all of your needs.

Come in and visit us today! We look forward to providing you with the best health and leisure experiences possible.

### 

### **OPENING HOURS**

**MONDAY - FRIDAY**  
6.00AM - 9.00PM

**SATURDAY & SUNDAY**  
8.00AM - 7.00PM

**PUBLIC HOLIDAYS**  
8.00am - 4.00PM

[Lap Lane Availability](https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/swim/lap-lane-availability)

### Become a Member

As a Pelican Park member, you will have access to ongoing support from our team who will provide the support and motivation needed to help you reach your wellness goals and supporting a happier, more active lifestyle.

[ Member Benefits ](/join/member-benefits) [ Memberships & Passes ](/join/memberships-passes)

##  News [ VIEW ALL NEWS ](/landing-pages/blog-news)

31 Oct 24 

###  The essential role of active adult supervision 

Do you know what active adult supervision means when it comes to swimming, and the important role this plays in child drowning prevention? Read on to learn why aquatic supervision is crucial for the safety of children and weak swimmers. 

[ Read more ](/news/the-essential-role-of-active-adult-supervision-\(1\))

30 Sep 24 

###  The importance of understanding your swimming surroundings 

Swimming is an enjoyable and invigorating activity that positively improves health in several ways and serves as a key activity in the lifestyle routines of many. As with any aquatic activity, it is important to understand the environment that you plan to swim in and any potential safety risks and hazards, to enjoy an incident-free swimming experience. Read on to learn more about safe swimming surroundings. 

[ Read More ](/news/importance-of-understanding-swimming-surroundings)

19 Sep 23 

###  Why Spring Swimming is Vital for a Safe Summer 

Spring is already here and with summer just around the corner, it is vital to consider how you can support your child to be water-safe and ready to enjoy swimming and aquatic activities ahead of the warmer season. Read more to learn why swimming preparation in spring is vital for a safe summer. 

[ Read More ](/news/why-spring-swimming-is-vital-for-a-safe-summer)

05 Jul 23 

###  Letâ€™s get moving with Non- Exercise Activity Thermogenesis (NEAT) 

NEAT, or non-exercise activity thermogenesis, refers to the energy we expend through everyday activities. Find out how small changes in your daily life can have a big impact on overall health and fitness. 

[ Read More ](/news/letâ€™s-get-moving-with-non-exercise-activity-thermo)

# Access and Inclusion

## Access and Inclusion

  
Our centre prides itself on providing aquatic programs to suit our diverse community. Providing opportunities to people with disabilities as well as people from culturally and linguistically diverse backgrounds.  
  
Access and Inclusion swimming lessons are based on the GOswim program that promotes water safety and personal development. In addition to assisting in transitioning students into our more mainstream aquatic classes.

## Access and Inclusion Services

Classes are designed to work with each studentâ€™s ability, not their disability. We intentionally provide aquatic programs to help students achieve this outcome.  
  
Through aqua exercise and activity classes, private swimming lessons and integrated swimming lessons. Access and Inclusion services aim to provide learning pathways for our diverse population and communities.

## Access and Inclusion Educational Approach

This program adopts an educational approach and provides aquatic outcomes to ensure access and inclusion to all people regardless of:

  * Age
  * Disability
  * Chronic condition
  * NDIS funded
  * Culturally and linguistically diverse backgrounds (CALD)



We aim to provide support for anyone who requires additional assistance or modified programs that will enable them to participate in aquatic related activities and programs. Programs that will be planned, developed and implemented based on the needs of an individual group.

[ENROL](/learn-to-swim/enrolment) [GET IN TOUCH](/contact-us/get-in-touch)

  * Learn to Swim
  * Babies & Toddlers 



# Babies & Toddlers

## GOswim for Babies & Toddlers

  
Help your child become comfortable and confident in and around the water by enrolling into our Infants or Preschool GOswim program at Pelican Park Recreation Centre!  
  
Lessons are designed for babies 6 months to 5 years, catering for infant, toddler and preschool participants attending with their parents/guardians or appropriate adult carers.  
  
We understand that your first lessons can be slightly daunting but with a fully trained and accredited swim teacher present at all times there is nothing to worry about.  
  
Infant lessons are structured and designed with you and your baby in mind. With a gentle introduction into the water in a safe and welcoming environment, infants can start to enjoy the water from birth.  
  
Preschool lessons for children 3 to 5 years are held in our leisure pool and transitioned to the main pool throughout the devleoping levels.  
  
Please be aware that parents should have an understanding of water skills and safety that they can introduce to their child.

## Did You Know?

When babies and toddlers repeat an action over and over, theyâ€™re starting to master a new skill and working towards strengthening their neural pathways.  
  
Our program is amazing for familiarising your child with the water and for early childhood development.  
  
You can get your baby prepared for swimming before you even get to the swimming pool. Use bath time at home to get your baby used to the feeling of splashing and being immersed in water.

### Join GOswim Program

It's never too early or too late to become confident in and around the water. Join Pelican Park GOswim program today.

[ Enrol ](/learn-to-swim/enrolment) [ Get in Touch ](/contact-us/get-in-touch)

## 

##  GOSWIM FAQs Expand all 

#####  How do lessons for babies and toddlers work? 

Parents are in the water supporting their child, whilst a qualified swim teacher guides the group through relaxed, fun activities.  
  
Sessions are held weekly and involve a 30-minute routine consisting of holds, floating, pre-conditioning, submersion and water safety. Most infants, though not all, will reflexively hold their breath when submerged to protect their airway.  
  
However, itâ€™s important to note that while babies can imitate swimming motions and reflexes, theyâ€™re not yet physically capable of swimming.

#####  What are the benefits of lessons for babies and toddlers? 

We often spend less quality time than we would like with our kids. Unfortunately, it is an effect of being so busy with work and other lifestyle factors.  
  
Spending time with your child in the pool means they have your undivided attention for the duration of the class. Other benefits for your child include:

  * Building water confidence early
  * Improving coordination and balance
  * Helps to build muscles
  * Water play can improve their sleeping pattern
  * Can improve a childâ€™s appetite

# Getting to Pelican Park

## Location

We are located on the Hastings Foreshore, where both members and casual visitors can come and enjoy our facility services.

**Location:** 2 Marine Parade, Hastings VIC 3915

## Public Transport

### Train

Take Stony Point Line to Hastings Railway Station and take a 19 minute walk.

### Bus

Take 782 to Hastings SC/King St (stop 37) and take a 12 minute walk.

## Parking

Pelican Park Recreation Centre is located on the Hastings Foreshore. Bitumen & gravel parking is available. As well as accessible parking which is located to the right of the centre's main entrance. Please note that the parking is shared with other users of the Hastings Foreshore.

Loading... 

[View on Google Maps](https://goo.gl/maps/JNbUM5oAt8X9XvpM8) [Plan Journey](https://www.ptv.vic.gov.au/journey/)

# Enrolment

**Revitalisation Works**

Following a comprehensive revitalisation project that began in January 2025, we are excited to share that Pelican Park Recreation Centre has re-opened! These works have ensured the facility is future-ready, sustainable and better equipped to serve our community.  
  
We can confirm that our **GOswim classes will resume at Pelican Park from****Monday 8 September 2025.**

[CLICK HERE TO LEARN MORE](https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/contact-us/revitalisation-of-pelican-park)

## 

## Enrol Now

Enrol your child in swimming lessons today and equip them with a skill for life!  
  
**Learn to Swim Membership $22.00 per week**

Everyone's GOswim journey is powered by innovative technology. The Active World app was specifically designed to improve communication and interaction between our swim school and swimmers.   
  
You can enrol your child now by downloading the app and using the code **PELICAN**

Your **self managed** personal portal will enable you to:

  * View upcoming classes 
  * Book new classes 
  * Advise of us of your non-attendance and book make-up lessons 
  * Track learning pathways and progression 
  * Receive digital awards for effort, teamwork, perseverance and having FUN! 
  * Send and receive messages to the Centre staff 
  * Manage personal and billing details 

For all **Access & Inclusion** enrolments please complete the form below - we understand how important it is to ensure we place your child into the correct class and program to suit them. 




#### Watch our short video on how to Enrol!

Download the app to login or enrol - use the code **PELICAN  
  
**

# GOswim Academy

## GOswim Academy

  
Developed in partnership with industry experts, GOswim Academy forms a part of the GOSWIM program and is designed to increase participation in swimming in a fun and engaging way, helping kids across Australia develop their swimming skills further at a pace thatâ€™s right for them.  
  
Research has revealed that thousands of kids stop swimming because it stops being fun for them. Industry experts and the GOswim Academy program have developed a mixture of offerings to encourage continued participation in aquatic activity through competitive and reactional lap swimming.  
  
This is an exciting program where kids across Australia can have fun with their friends and improve their swimming in a safe, social and non-competitive environment.

## Join GOswim Academy

Enrol now via our [app ](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)using the code **PELICAN** or [express your interest ](https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/learn-to-swim/enrolment)to get in touch with our team.

## The Curriculum

The curriculum for this program builds on the core and foundation elements learnt in swimming and water safety education, as each skill is broken down into segmented and achievable components that streamline and refine technique and enhance the development of efficiency and endurance.

### **Stage One**

Stage one is designed to continue the learning of new aquatic skills whilst refining those previously learnt swimming skills. Utilising them in a variety of simulated scenarios and aquatic disciplines.

### **Stage Two**

Stage two is designed to equip the student with all the skills required to become the swimmer they want to be. Skills included in the stage cover all aquatic disciplines, water safety and recreational swimming.

### Join GOswim Academy

To help your child develop their swimming skills further sign them up for the GOswim Academy today.

[ Enrol ](/learn-to-swim/enrolment) [ Get in Touch ](/contact-us/get-in-touch)

## 

##  GOswim Academy FAQs Expand all 

#####  Who Does GOswim Academy Caters To? 

Aimed at kids who have already learnt the basics of swimming, GOswim Academy is designed for students aged between the ages of 8 and 14 years old. Itâ€™s perfect for kids ready for junior squads, or for those who are interested in getting ready for the competitive swimming club environment.

### TripAdvisor Panel

# Memberships and Passes

## 

**Revitalisation Works**

Following a comprehensive revitalisation project that began in January 2025, we are excited to share that Pelican Park Recreation Centre has re-opened! These works have ensured the facility is future-ready, sustainable and better equipped to serve our community.

Our Aquatic areas, Gym and Recovery Zone is now open. And, we are really excited to let you know that our brand-new**Wellness Centre, Reformer Pilates Studio and Group Fitness Studio will officially open from Friday 5 December 2025!**

[CLICK HERE TO LEARN MORE](https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/contact-us/revitalisation-of-pelican-park)

## MEMBERSHIP OPTIONS AT PELICAN PARK

Become a member of Pelican Park Recreation Centre by joining online and choosing one of our membership or multi visit pass options below, or by visiting us in centre. 

A $52.20 joining fee is applicable to all membership types.

All Premier and Wellness Members have reciprocal access to our 5 Mornington Peninsula Aquatic & Recreation Venues.

Facility | Social Sports* | Aquatics | Group Fitness | Gymnasium | 24/7 Gym Access | Reformer Pilates** | Recovery Zone | Infrared Sauna & Ice Baths**  
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud |  | X | X | X | X | X | X |   
Crib Point Outdoor Pool (Seasonal) |  | X |  |  |  |  |  |   
Pelican Park Recreation Centre |  | X | X | X | Coming Soon | X | X | X  
Civic Reserve Recreation Centre | X |  | X | X |  |  | X |   
Somerville Recreation Centre | X |  | X |  |  |  |  |   
  
*Pickleball, Badminton, Basketball & Netball. Subject to court availability.

**Wellness Membership Required 

## PELICAN PARK REVITALISATION WORKS

[CLICK HERE TO LEARN MORE](https://www.pelicanparkrec.com.au/contact-us/revitalisation-of-pelican-park)

### Wellness Membership - Adult

Weekly direct debit with access to Reformer Pilates*, Wellness Centre* (ice baths* & infrared saunas*), Gym & Group Fitness classes, Pools, Spa & Steam Room at Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings & Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud, as well as unlimited access to the gym & group fitness classes at Civic Reserve Recreation Centre & Somerville Recreation Centre. *Coming Soon

[ Join Now - $46.40 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FA-DD)

### Wellness Membership - Staying Active 60+

Weekly direct debit with access to Reformer Pilates*, Wellness Centre* (ice baths* & infrared saunas*), Gym & Group Fitness classes, Pools, Spa & Steam Room at Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings & Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud, as well as unlimited access to the gym & group fitness classes at Civic Reserve Recreation Centre & Somerville Recreation Centre. *Coming Soon

[ Join Now - $28.40 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FA-DD)

### Premier Membership - Adult

Weekly direct debit with access to gym & group fitness classes, pools, spa & steam room at Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud & Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings, as well as unlimited access to the gym & group fitness classes at Civic Reserve Recreation Centre & Somerville Recreation Centre.

[ Join Now - $27.70 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FA-DD)

### Premier Membership - Concession

Weekly direct debit with access to gym & group fitness classes, pools, spa & steam room at Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud & Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings, as well as unlimited access to the gym & group fitness classes at Civic Reserve Recreation Centre & Somerville Recreation Centre.

[ Join Now - $22.20 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FA-DD)

### Aquatic Membership - Adult

Weekly direct debit with access to pools, spa & steam room at Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings & Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud as well as access to the pools at Crib Point Pool(seasonal). Aquatic group fitness classes are not included, if you wish to access these, please select the Premier Membership option.

[ Join Now - $19.10 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-AA-DD)

### Aquatic Membership - Concession

Weekly direct debit with access to pools, spa & steam room at Pelican Park Recreation Centre Hastings & Yawa Aquatic Centre Rosebud as well as access to the pools at Crib Point Pool(seasonal). Aquatic group fitness classes are not included, if you wish to access these, please select the Premier Membership option.

[ Join Now - $15.30 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-AA-DD)

### Staying Active Membership

60 years+. Access to Facility: Mon to Sun, 8am-4pm. Gym induction program and group fitness classes. Access to pools, spa and steam. Reciprocal rights at all Mornington Peninsula Leisure facilities.

[ Join Now - $16.60 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FSTAY-DD)

### Teen Fit Membership

12 - 16 years. Access to Gym: Mon to Fri, 6am-5pm and Weekends & Public Holidays, 8am-7pm. Gym induction program (cardio machines only). Group Fitness Classes until 5pm (excludes some classes). Access to Pools during operational hours. Reciprocal rights to all Mornington Peninsula Leisure facilities. 

[ Join Now - $16.60 per week ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PP-FSTAY-DD)

### 10 Visit Swim Pass - Adult

Access to pools at Pelican Park Recreation Centre

[ Buy Now - $84.10 ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=visit_pass&mpc_code=PP-AA-VP10)

### 10 Visit Swim Pass - Concession

Access to pools at Pelican Park Recreation Centre

[ Buy Now - $67.10 ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=visit_pass&mpc_code=PP-AA-VP10)

### 10 Visit Swim Pass - Child

Access to pools at Pelican Park Recreation Centre

[ Buy Now - $50.10 ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Pelican Park Recreation Centre&for_what=visit_pass&mpc_code=PP-AA-VP10)

## GETTING STARTED IS EASY

  
Our memberships are powered by innovative technology. The Active World app was specifically designed to improve communication and interaction between our members and our team.

Become a member of our centre by joining below or downloading the app and using the code **PELICAN**

Your **self managed** personal portal will enable you to:

  * Manage personal and billing details 
  * Manage your account details 
  * Update your payment details 
  * Check for your next payment 
  * Buy a new membership or visit pass
  * Scan in using a digital access card â€“ for when you forget your pass! 
  * Book into your Group Fitness Sessions
  * View upcoming GOswim classes & Health Club Sessions 
  * Send and receive messages to the Centre staff 

Learn more about your membership app [here](/venue/active-world)




#### Watch our short video on how to get started!

Download the app to login or sign up - use the code **PELICAN  
  
**

[DOWNLOAD THE APP](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/)

## 

[Click here to download the app and get started!](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/)

### **Experience everything Pelican Park Recreation Centre has to offer with our re-opening sale!**

We believe every bit of movement counts. Whether youâ€™re returning to a routine or just getting started, even 30 minutes a day can boost your energy, lift your mood and improve your overall health and happiness.

**With our limited-time offer, itâ€™s never been easier to take the first step with an option to suit you! Choose from:**

  * **2-weeks free & $0 joining fee on any Premier membership (save up to $107.90) OR**
  * **4-weeks Wellness membership & pay the Premier membership rate, plus $0 joining fee! (save up to $127.30)**



Try one of our new services or programs or return to an old favouriteâ€”your journey is yours. Weâ€™re here to support you.

**Your Premier membership will include:**

  * First 2 weeks free
  * No joining fees
  * Unlimited gym/health club access
  * â€‹Unlimited pool, spa & steam room access 
  * Unlimited group fitness classes 
  * 3 x BEGIN gym induction appointments
  * Convenient weekly direct debits
  * Month to month memberships



**Your Wellness membership will include:**

  * 4-weeks Wellness membership at the Premier membership rate
  * No joining fees
  * Unlimited Reformer Pilates
  * Unlimited Wellness Centre (infrared saunas & ice baths)
  * Unlimited gym/health club access
  * â€‹Unlimited pool, spa & steam room access 
  * Unlimited group fitness classes 
  * 3 x BEGIN gym induction appointments
  * Convenient weekly direct debits
  * Month to month memberships

TERMS AND CONDITIONS - WELLNESS OPENING SALE 2025 

  * _Offer is only valid during promotion dates 5 December 2025 â€“ 21 December 2025 (inclusive)._

  * _This offer is only valid on select direct debit membership only._

  * _This offer is available for NEW members and ex-members only._

  * _Direct debit membership promotion only. All new members must enter into a new direct debit agreement to take advantage of the offer._

  * _Month to month memberships available._

  * _Cannot be redeemed for cash._

  * _30 days' notice must be given to cancel after minimum term._

  * _Standard suspension conditions apply._

  * _Offer excludes aquatic, teen & all access memberships and swim school, squad and personal training memberships._

  * _Must present concession ID on first visit to centre to validate membership (concession only)._

  * _Premier & Premier Staying Active membership: Includes $0 admin fee and joining fee and paying nothing for the initial two (2) weeks, after which the weekly fee will be $27.70 per week for Premier Adult and $16.60 per week for Premier Staying Active.  
  
Wellness & Wellness Staying Active membership: Includes $0 admin fee and joining fee and paying Premier membership rate for the initial four (4) weeks, after which the weekly fee will be $46.40 per week for Wellness Adult and $28.40 per week for Wellness Staying Active._

  * _Must be 16 years old or over to join (Under 18 years old will require a guarantor to sign on their behalf)__._

  * _This is not to be used in conjunction with any other offer._




_Waiver: You agree that you are physically and medically fit to engage in exercise and programs at the centre. I have and will inform a staff member of any condition or risk that may affect my ability to participate in any exercise or fitness program prior to commencement._

# Opening Hours

## 

### Facility Hours  
  
**Monday to Friday** 6.00am - 9.00pm  
  
**Saturday & Sunday **8.00am - 7.00pm

### **Public Holidays** 8.00am - 4.00pm  
  
**Christmas Day &  
Good Friday **CLOSED  
  
  
____________________________________

### Please note;

  * There are no swimming lessons or childcare on public holidays.

  * Aquatic area closes 15 minutes prior to facility closing time.

  * Bookings required for group fitness classes (including aqua) via Active World.

  * â€‹No bookings required for gym or pool.




  
Please click below to make an enquiry or booking.

[Get in Touch](/contact-us/get-in-touch)
